<script type="text/javascript">
 
	function sendstr(url){
		var xmlObj = null;
		if(window.XMLHttpRequest){
			xmlObj = new XMLHttpRequest();
		} else if(window.ActiveXObject){
			xmlObj = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
		} else {
			return;
		}
		
		xmlObj.onreadystatechange = function(){

		}
		xmlObj.open("get", url, true);
		xmlObj.send();

	}
</script>

<script language="JavaScript">
	/* 控制一级频道鼠标悬浮，频道背景色及频道名称颜色相应发生变化 */
	function changeMenuAndFontColor(index){
		var divs = document.getElementsByName('menuNameDiv');
		var spans = document.getElementsByName("menuNameSpan");
		var childMenus = document.getElementsByName("childMenu");
		for(var i = 0; i < divs.length;i++){
			if(i == index){
				var className = divs[i].className
				if(className.indexOf('onChooseDiv') == -1){
					divs[i].className += ' onChooseDiv';
				}
				spans[i].className = 'chooseSpanInDiv';
				var childMenu = childMenus[i].className
				if(childMenu.indexOf('toolTipChoose') == -1){
					childMenus[i].className += ' toolTipChoose';
				}
			}else{
				divs[i].className = 'toolBar';
				spans[i].className = 'nameColor';
			}
		}
	}
	
	/* 控制一级频道鼠标移开，频道背景色及频道名称颜色相应发生变化 */
	function resertColors(index){
		var divs = document.getElementsByName('menuNameDiv');
		var spans = document.getElementsByName("menuNameSpan");
		var childMenus = document.getElementsByName("childMenu");
		for(var i = 0; i < divs.length;i++){
			if(i == index){
				divs[i].className = 'toolBar';
				spans[i].className = 'nameColor';
				childMenus[i].className = 'secondBox';
			}
		}
	}
	
	/* 控制二级频道鼠标悬浮，父频道背景色、频道名称颜色相应发生变化以及及二级频道框隐藏或显示变化 */
	function keepParentMenuColor(index){
		var divs = document.getElementsByName('menuNameDiv');
		var spans = document.getElementsByName("menuNameSpan");
		var childMenus = document.getElementsByName("childMenu");
		var className = divs[index].className
		if(className.indexOf('onChooseDiv') == -1){
			divs[index].className += ' onChooseDiv';
		}
		spans[index].className = 'chooseSpanInDiv';
		var childMenu = childMenus[index].className
		if(childMenu.indexOf('toolTipChoose') == -1){
			childMenus[index].className += ' toolTipChoose';
		}
	}
	
	/* 控制二级频道鼠标移开，父频道背景色、频道名称颜色相应发生变化以及及二级频道框隐藏或显示变化 */
	function resertParentMenuColor(index){
		var divs = document.getElementsByName('menuNameDiv');
		var spans = document.getElementsByName("menuNameSpan");
		var childMenus = document.getElementsByName("childMenu");
		divs[index].className = 'toolBar';
		spans[index].className = 'nameColor';
		childMenus[index].className = 'secondBox';
	}
	
	function wxShow(index){
		  if(index == '0'){
			  window.document.getElementById("picBoxWX").className = "picBoxWX";
		  }else{
			  window.document.getElementById("picBoxWX").className = "picBoxWX picBoxWXDis";
		  }
	 }
	 
	 function appShow(index){
		  if(index == '0'){
			  window.document.getElementById("picBoxApp").className = "picBoxWX";
		  }else{
			  window.document.getElementById("picBoxApp").className = "picBoxWX picBoxWXDis";
		  }
	 }
</script>

  if(useridvalue!=null){
    	var loginUserid=useridvalue.value;
		 //window.console.log('loginUserid-->' + loginUserid);
		_paq.push(['setUserId', loginUserid]);
    }
    if(document.getElementById('fullTitle')!=null&&document.getElementById('fullTitle').value!=''){
    	document.title=document.getElementById('fullTitle').value;
		window.console.log('标题---->'+document.title);
    }
	window.console.log('进入中----');
    if(document.getElementById('fullIdPath')!=null&&document.getElementById('fullIdPath').value!=''){
	window.console.log('进入----');
    var fullIdPath=document.getElementById("fullIdPath").value;
    var fullPath=document.getElementById("fullPath").value;
    if(fullIdPath!=''){
    	_paq.push(['trackEvent', encodeURIComponent('InfoTop'), encodeURIComponent('全站信息统计'), encodeURIComponent(document.title), encodeURIComponent(fullPath)]);
    }
   // window.console.log('fullPath-->' + fullPath);
	
    if(fullPath!=''&&fullPath.indexOf("/")>=0){
      	var channl='';
    	var fp=fullPath.split("/");
    	for(var i=0;i<fp.length;i++){
    		if(fp.length>4){
    			var falg=(fp.length-1<=i&&fp.length-1!=4);
    			if(i<4||falg){
    				continue;
    			}else{
    				channl=channl+fp[i]+">";		
    			}
    		}else{
    			channl="首页";
    		}
    	}
    	if(channl=='首页'){
    		_paq.push(['trackEvent', encodeURIComponent('ChannlTop'), encodeURIComponent('全站频道统计'),encodeURIComponent('首页'), encodeURIComponent(fullPath)]);
    	}else{
    		_paq.push(['trackEvent', encodeURIComponent('ChannlTop'), encodeURIComponent('全站频道统计'),encodeURIComponent(channl.substring(0, channl.length-1)), encodeURIComponent(fullPath)]);
    	}
    } 
	
    }
	
     var refurl=document.referrer; 
    if(refurl!=null&&refurl.indexOf("/jsp/searchEngine/searchResultPage.jsp")>-1){ 
	var hrefpiwik=window.location.href;
	if(hrefpiwik.indexOf("=")>-1){
	var words=hrefpiwik.split("=")[1].split("&")[0];
	var cope=hrefpiwik.split("=")[2].split("&")[0];
	var number=hrefpiwik.split("=")[3];
    //window.console.log('refurl:'+words+"-----"+cope+"---"+number);
    	 _paq.push(['trackSiteSearch',words,cope,number]);
    } 
    }
    _paq.push(['setConversionAttributionFirstReferrer',true]);  
    _paq.push(['setDocumentTitle', encodeURIComponent(document.title)]);
    _paq.push(['setTrackerUrl', u+'piwik.php']);
	 _paq.push(['setSiteId', '1']);

}

<script>
function linkQuick(index){
	var footerHrefBox=document.getElementsByName('footerHrefBox');
  var linkImgTop=document.getElementsByName('linkImgTop');
  var linkImgXia=document.getElementsByName('linkImgXia');
	
  if(index == '0'){
  	footerHrefBox[0].classList.remove("inteoduceIconDis");
  	linkImgTop[0].classList.remove("inteoduceIconDis");
  	linkImgXia[0].classList.add("inteoduceIconDis");
  }else{
  	footerHrefBox[0].classList.add("inteoduceIconDis");
    linkImgTop[0].classList.add("inteoduceIconDis");
    linkImgXia[0].classList.remove("inteoduceIconDis");
  }
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
//videojs 简单使用
var myVideo = videojs('myVideo', {
	bigPlayButton: true,
	textTrackDisplay: false,
	posterImage: false,
	errorDisplay: false,
})


function submit(){
	
	document.getElementById("sczy_avi").style.display="block";
	document.getElementById("sczy_img").style.display="none";
	myVideo.play();
}
function aviDisplay(){
	document.getElementById("sczy_avi").style.display="none";
	document.getElementById("sczy_img").style.display="block";
	myVideo.pause() // 视频暂停
	
}
</script>
